             <h6 class="zsg-subfooter-header">
              Why use Zillow?
             </h6>
             <p>
              Zillow is perfect for searching homes for sale in the United States. By analyzing real estate information on millions of homes for sale across the United States, we calculate home values (Zestimates) and the Zillow Home Value Price Index.

                      </a>
                      to make the Zestimate more accurate. Plus, you can leave an opinion on your Zestimate value below. Just click "Owner Estimate".

            <section class="zsg-content-section collapsible collapsed" id="hdp-neighborhood">
             <h2>
              Neighborhood: 52214
             </h2>
             <div class="zsg-content-component">
              <div class="za-track-event zsg-content-component notranslate" data-za-action="Market Guide - expand" data-za-category="Homes">
               Zillow predicts Central City home values will increase 2.2% next year, compared to a 2% rise for Cedar Rapids Metro as a whole. Among Central City homes, this home is valued 26.2% less than the midpoint (median) home, and is valued 50% less per square foot.
               <br/>
               <br/>
               Foreclosures will be a factor impacting home values in the next several years.  In Central City, the number of foreclosures waiting to be sold is 25% lower than in Cedar Rapids Metro, and 97.1% less than the national average. This lower local number could help Central City home values rise more quickly than other regions in Cedar Rapids Metro.
               <br/>
               <br/>
               Learn more about
               <a href="https://zillow.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/203517190-How-are-Zillow-Home-Value-Forecasts-calculated-">
                forecast calculations
               </a>
               or
               <a href="http://www.zillow.com/central-city-ia/home-values/">
                Central City home values
               </a>
               .
